### zoonotic-disease.html

**Heading Issues:**
- Heading hierarchy skip: jumped from H1 to H3

## Recommendations

1. **Heading Hierarchy**: Ensure headings follow a logical hierarchy without skipping levels.
2. **SVG Alt Text**: Add `aria-label` attributes to SVG diagrams describing their content.
3. **Image Alt Text**: Ensure all images have meaningful alt text for screen readers.
4. **Table Headers**: Add `scope` attributes to `<th>` elements to identify header relationships.
5. **Scripts**: Review inline scripts for security implications. Consider moving to external files.
